    27	//! Aggregate Function packages for [DataFusion].
    28	//!
    29	//! This crate contains a collection of various aggregate function packages for DataFusion,
    30	//! implemented using the extension API. Users may wish to control which functions
    31	//! are available to control the binary size of their application as well as
    32	//! use dialect specific implementations of functions (e.g. Spark vs Postgres)
    33	//!
    34	//! Each package is implemented as a separate
    35	//! module, activated by a feature flag.
    36	//!
    37	//! [DataFusion]: https://crates.io/crates/datafusion
    38	//!
    39	//! # Available Packages
    40	//! See the list of [modules](#modules) in this crate for available packages.
    41	//!
    42	//! # Using A Package
    43	//! You can register all functions in all packages using the [`register_all`] function.
    44	//!
    45	//! Each package also exports an `expr_fn` submodule to help create [`Expr`]s that invoke
    46	//! functions using a fluent style. For example:
    47	//!
    48	//![`Expr`]: datafusion_expr::Expr
    49	//!
    50	//! # Implementing A New Package
    51	//!
    52	//! To add a new package to this crate, you should follow the model of existing
    53	//! packages. The high level steps are:
    54	//!
    55	//! 1. Create a new module with the appropriate [AggregateUDF] implementations.
    56	//!
    57	//! 2. Use the macros in [`macros`] to create standard entry points.
    58	//!
    59	//! 3. Add a new feature to `Cargo.toml`, with any optional dependencies
    60	//!
    61	//! 4. Use the `make_package!` macro to expose the module when the
    62	//!    feature is enabled.
    63	
    64	#[macro_use]
    65	pub mod macros;
    66

   177	        bool_and_or::bool_or_udaf(),
   178	        average::avg_udaf(),
   179	        grouping::grouping_udaf(),
   180	        nth_value::nth_value_udaf(),
   181	    ]
   182	}
   183	
   184	/// Registers all enabled packages with a [`FunctionRegistry`]
   185	pub fn register_all(registry: &mut dyn FunctionRegistry) -> Result<()> {
   186	    let functions: Vec<Arc<AggregateUDF>> = all_default_aggregate_functions();
   187	
   188	    functions.into_iter().try_for_each(|udf| {
   189	        let existing_udaf = registry.register_udaf(udf)?;
   190	        if let Some(existing_udaf) = existing_udaf {
   191	            debug!("Overwrite existing UDAF: {}", existing_udaf.name());
   192	        }
   193	        Ok(()) as Result<()>
   194	    })?;
   195	
   196	    Ok(())
   197	}
   198

    21	use std::ops::Deref;

    23	
    24	/// A wrapper around a pointer to UDF that implements `Eq` and `Hash` delegating to
    25	/// corresponding methods on the UDF trait.
    26	///
    27	/// If you want to just compare pointers for equality, use [`super::ptr_eq::PtrEq`].
    28	#[derive(Clone)]
    29	#[allow(private_bounds)] // This is so that UdfEq can only be used with allowed pointer types (e.g. Arc), without allowing misuse.
    30	pub struct UdfEq<Ptr: UdfPointer>(Ptr);
    31	
    32	impl<Ptr> PartialEq for UdfEq<Ptr>
    33	where
    34	    Ptr: UdfPointer,
    35	{
    36	    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
    37	        self.0.equals(&other.0)
    38	    }
    39	}
    40	impl<Ptr> Eq for UdfEq<Ptr> where Ptr: UdfPointer {}
    41	impl<Ptr> Hash for UdfEq<Ptr>
    42	where
    43	    Ptr: UdfPointer,
    44	{
    45	    fn hash<H: Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
    46	        self.0.hash_value().hash(state);
    47	    }
    48	}
    49	
    50	impl<Ptr> From<Ptr> for UdfEq<Ptr>
    51	where
    52	    Ptr: UdfPointer,
    53	{
    54	    fn from(ptr: Ptr) -> Self {
    55	        UdfEq(ptr)
    56	    }
    57	}
    58	
    59	impl<Ptr> Debug for UdfEq<Ptr>
    60	where
    61	    Ptr: UdfPointer + Debug,
    62	{
    63	    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
    64	        self.0.fmt(f)
    65	    }
    66	}
    67	
    68	impl<Ptr> Deref for UdfEq<Ptr>
    69	where
    70	    Ptr: UdfPointer,
    71	{
    72	    type Target = Ptr;
    73	
    74	    fn deref(&self) -> &Self::Target {
    75	        &self.0
    76	    }
    77	}
    78	
    79	trait UdfPointer: Deref {
    80	    fn equals(&self, other: &Self::Target) -> bool;
    81	    fn hash_value(&self) -> u64;
    82	}
    83	
    84	macro_rules! impl_for_udf_eq {
    85	    ($udf:ty) => {
    86	        impl UdfPointer for Arc<$udf> {
    87	            fn equals(&self, other: &$udf) -> bool {
    88	                self.as_ref().equals(other)
    89	            }
    90	
    91	            fn hash_value(&self) -> u64 {
    92	                self.as_ref().hash_value()
    93	            }
    94	        }
    95	    };
    96	}
    97	
    98	impl_for_udf_eq!(dyn AggregateUDFImpl + '_);
    99	impl_for_udf_eq!(dyn ScalarUDFImpl + '_);
   100	
   101	impl UdfPointer for Arc<dyn WindowUDFImpl + '_> {
   102	    fn equals(&self, other: &(dyn WindowUDFImpl + '_)) -> bool {
   103	        self.as_ref().dyn_eq(other.as_any())
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    fn hash_value(&self) -> u64 {
   107	        let hasher = &mut DefaultHasher::new();
   108	        self.as_ref().dyn_hash(hasher);
   109	        hasher.finish()
   110	    }
   111	}

   157	    pub fn test_eq_eq_wrapper() {
   158	        let signature = Signature::any(1, Volatility::Immutable);
   159	
   160	        let a1: Arc<dyn ScalarUDFImpl> = Arc::new(TestScalarUDF {
   161	            signature: signature.clone(),
   162	            name: "a",
   163	        });
   164	        let a2: Arc<dyn ScalarUDFImpl> = Arc::new(TestScalarUDF {
   165	            signature: signature.clone(),
   166	            name: "a",
   167	        });
   168	        let b: Arc<dyn ScalarUDFImpl> = Arc::new(TestScalarUDF {
   169	            signature: signature.clone(),
   170	            name: "b",
   171	        });
   172	
   173	        // Reflexivity
   174	        let wrapper = UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1));
   175	        assert_eq!(wrapper, wrapper);
   176	
   177	        // Two wrappers around equal pointer
   178	        assert_eq!(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1)), UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1)));
   179	        assert_eq!(hash(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1))), hash(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1))));
   180	
   181	        // Two wrappers around different pointers but equal in ScalarUDFImpl::equals sense
   182	        assert_eq!(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1)), UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a2)));
   183	        assert_eq!(hash(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1))), hash(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a2))));
   184	
   185	        // different functions (not equal)
   186	        assert_ne!(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1)), UdfEq(Arc::clone(&b)));
   187	    }

   191	        value.hash(hasher);
   192	        hasher.finish()
   193	    }

    47	/// Logical representation of a user-defined [aggregate function] (UDAF).
    48	///
    49	/// An aggregate function combines the values from multiple input rows
    50	/// into a single output "aggregate" (summary) row. It is different
    51	/// from a scalar function because it is stateful across batches. User
    52	/// defined aggregate functions can be used as normal SQL aggregate
    53	/// functions (`GROUP BY` clause) as well as window functions (`OVER`
    54	/// clause).
    55	///
    56	/// `AggregateUDF` provides DataFusion the information needed to plan and call
    57	/// aggregate functions, including name, type information, and a factory
    58	/// function to create an [`Accumulator`] instance, to perform the actual
    59	/// aggregation.
    60	///
    61	/// For more information, please see [the examples]:
    62	///
    63	/// 1. For simple use cases, use [`create_udaf`] (examples in [`simple_udaf.rs`]).
    64	///
    65	/// 2. For advanced use cases, use [`AggregateUDFImpl`] which provides full API
    66	///    access (examples in [`advanced_udaf.rs`]).
    67	///
    68	/// # API Note
    69	/// This is a separate struct from `AggregateUDFImpl` to maintain backwards
    70	/// compatibility with the older API.
    71	///
    72	/// [the examples]: https://github.com/apache/datafusion/tree/main/datafusion-examples#single-process
    73	/// [aggregate function]: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aggregate_function
    74	/// [`Accumulator`]: crate::Accumulator
    75	/// [`create_udaf`]: crate::expr_fn::create_udaf
    76	/// [`simple_udaf.rs`]: https://github.com/apache/datafusion/blob/main/datafusion-examples/examples/simple_udaf.rs
    77	/// [`advanced_udaf.rs`]: https://github.com/apache/datafusion/blob/main/datafusion-examples/examples/advanced_udaf.rs
    78	#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialOrd)]
    79	pub struct AggregateUDF {
    80	    inner: Arc<dyn AggregateUDFImpl>,
    81	}
    82	
    83	impl PartialEq for AggregateUDF {
    84	    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
    85	        self.inner.equals(other.inner.as_ref())
    86	    }
    87	}
    88	
    89	impl Eq for AggregateUDF {}
    90	
    91	impl Hash for AggregateUDF {
    92	    fn hash<H: Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
    93	        self.inner.hash_value().hash(state)
    94	    }
    95	}
    96	
    97	impl fmt::Display for AggregateUDF {

   103	/// Arguments passed to [`AggregateUDFImpl::value_from_stats`]
   104	#[derive(Debug)]
   105	pub struct StatisticsArgs<'a> {

   120	impl AggregateUDF {
   121	    /// Create a new `AggregateUDF` from a `[AggregateUDFImpl]` trait object
   122	    ///
   123	    /// Note this is the same as using the `From` impl (`AggregateUDF::from`)
   124	    pub fn new_from_impl<F>(fun: F) -> AggregateUDF
   125	    where
   126	        F: AggregateUDFImpl + 'static,
   127	    {
   128	        Self::new_from_shared_impl(Arc::new(fun))
   129	    }
   130	
   131	    /// Create a new `AggregateUDF` from a `[AggregateUDFImpl]` trait object
   132	    pub fn new_from_shared_impl(fun: Arc<dyn AggregateUDFImpl>) -> AggregateUDF {
   133	        Self { inner: fun }
   134	    }
   135	
   136	    /// Return the underlying [`AggregateUDFImpl`] trait object for this function
   137	    pub fn inner(&self) -> &Arc<dyn AggregateUDFImpl> {
   138	        &self.inner
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    /// Adds additional names that can be used to invoke this function, in
   142	    /// addition to `name`
   143	    ///
   144	    /// If you implement [`AggregateUDFImpl`] directly you should return aliases directly.
   145	    pub fn with_aliases(self, aliases: impl IntoIterator<Item = &'static str>) -> Self {
   146	        Self::new_from_impl(AliasedAggregateUDFImpl::new(
   147	            Arc::clone(&self.inner),
   148	            aliases,
   149	        ))
   150	    }
   151	
   152	    /// Creates an [`Expr`] that calls the aggregate function.
   153	    ///
   154	    /// This utility allows using the UDAF without requiring access to
   155	    /// the registry, such as with the DataFrame API.
   156	    pub fn call(&self, args: Vec<Expr>) -> Expr {
   157	        Expr::AggregateFunction(AggregateFunction::new_udf(
   158	            Arc::new(self.clone()),
   159	            args,
   160	            false,
   161	            None,
   162	            vec![],
   163	            None,
   164	        ))
   165	    }

   345	impl<F> From<F> for AggregateUDF

   353	
   354	/// Trait for implementing [`AggregateUDF`].
   355	///
   356	/// This trait exposes the full API for implementing user defined aggregate functions and
   357	/// can be used to implement any function.
   358	///
   359	/// See [`advanced_udaf.rs`] for a full example with complete implementation and
   360	/// [`AggregateUDF`] for other available options.
   361	///
   362	/// [`advanced_udaf.rs`]: https://github.com/apache/datafusion/blob/main/datafusion-examples/examples/advanced_udaf.rs
   363	///
   364	/// # Basic Example
   365	/// ```
   366	/// # use std::any::Any;
   367	/// # use std::sync::{Arc, LazyLock};
   368	/// # use arrow::datatypes::{DataType, FieldRef};
   369	/// # use datafusion_common::{DataFusionError, plan_err, Result};
   370	/// # use datafusion_expr::{col, ColumnarValue, Signature, Volatility, Expr, Documentation};
   371	/// # use datafusion_expr::{AggregateUDFImpl, AggregateUDF, Accumulator, function::{AccumulatorArgs, StateFieldsArgs}};
   372	/// # use datafusion_expr::window_doc_sections::DOC_SECTION_AGGREGATE;
   373	/// # use arrow::datatypes::Schema;
   374	/// # use arrow::datatypes::Field;
   375	///
   376	/// #[derive(Debug, Clone)]
   377	/// struct GeoMeanUdf {
   378	///   signature: Signature,
   379	/// }
   380	///
   381	/// impl GeoMeanUdf {
   382	///   fn new() -> Self {
   383	///     Self {
   384	///       signature: Signature::uniform(1, vec![DataType::Float64], Volatility::Immutable),
   385	///      }
   386	///   }
   387	/// }
   388	///
   389	/// static DOCUMENTATION: LazyLock<Documentation> = LazyLock::new(|| {
   390	///         Documentation::builder(DOC_SECTION_AGGREGATE, "calculates a geometric mean", "geo_mean(2.0)")
   391	///             .with_argument("arg1", "The Float64 number for the geometric mean")
   392	///             .build()
   393	///     });
   394	///
   395	/// fn get_doc() -> &'static Documentation {
   396	///     &DOCUMENTATION
   397	/// }
   398	///
   399	/// /// Implement the AggregateUDFImpl trait for GeoMeanUdf
   400	/// impl AggregateUDFImpl for GeoMeanUdf {
   401	///    fn as_any(&self) -> &dyn Any { self }
   402	///    fn name(&self) -> &str { "geo_mean" }
   403	///    fn signature(&self) -> &Signature { &self.signature }
   404	///    fn return_type(&self, args: &[DataType]) -> Result<DataType> {
   405	///      if !matches!(args.get(0), Some(&DataType::Float64)) {
   406	///        return plan_err!("geo_mean only accepts Float64 arguments");
   407	///      }
   408	///      Ok(DataType::Float64)
   409	///    }
   410	///    // This is the accumulator factory; DataFusion uses it to create new accumulators.
   411	///    fn accumulator(&self, _acc_args: AccumulatorArgs) -> Result<Box<dyn Accumulator>> { unimplemented!() }
   412	///    fn state_fields(&self, args: StateFieldsArgs) -> Result<Vec<FieldRef>> {
   413	///        Ok(vec![
   414	///             Arc::new(args.return_field.as_ref().clone().with_name("value")),
   415	///             Arc::new(Field::new("ordering", DataType::UInt32, true))
   416	///        ])
   417	///    }
   418	///    fn documentation(&self) -> Option<&Documentation> {
   419	///        Some(get_doc())
   420	///    }
   421	/// }
   422	///
   423	/// // Create a new AggregateUDF from the implementation
   424	/// let geometric_mean = AggregateUDF::from(GeoMeanUdf::new());
   425	///
   426	/// // Call the function `geo_mean(col)`
   427	/// let expr = geometric_mean.call(vec![col("a")]);
   428	/// ```
   429	pub trait AggregateUDFImpl: Debug + Send + Sync {
   430	    /// Returns this object as an [`Any`] trait object
   431	    fn as_any(&self) -> &dyn Any;
   432	
   433	    /// Returns this function's name
   434	    fn name(&self) -> &str;
   435	
   436	    /// Returns any aliases (alternate names) for this function.
   437	    ///
   438	    /// Note: `aliases` should only include names other than [`Self::name`].
   439	    /// Defaults to `[]` (no aliases)
   440	    fn aliases(&self) -> &[String] {
   441	        &[]
   442	    }
   443	
   444	    /// Returns the name of the column this expression would create
   445	    ///
   446	    /// See [`Expr::schema_name`] for details
   447	    ///
   448	    /// Example of schema_name: count(DISTINCT column1) <response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you.    920	    /// *Must* be implemented explicitly if the UDF type has internal state.
   921	    /// Must be consistent with [`Self::hash_value`] and follow the same rules as [`Eq`]:
   922	    ///
   923	    /// - reflexive: `a.equals(a)`;
   924	    /// - symmetric: `a.equals(b)` implies `b.equals(a)`;
   925	    /// - transitive: `a.equals(b)` and `b.equals(c)` implies `a.equals(c)`.
   926	    ///
   927	    /// By default, compares type, [`Self::name`], [`Self::aliases`] and [`Self::signature`].
   928	    fn equals(&self, other: &dyn AggregateUDFImpl) -> bool {
   929	        self.as_any().type_id() == other.as_any().type_id()
   930	            && self.name() == other.name()
   931	            && self.aliases() == other.aliases()
   932	            && self.signature() == other.signature()
   933	    }
   934	
   935	    /// Returns a hash value for this aggregate UDF.
   936	    ///
   937	    /// Allows customizing the hash code of aggregate UDFs.
   938	    /// *Must* be implemented explicitly whenever [`Self::equals`] is implemented.
   939	    ///
   940	    /// Similarly to [`Hash`] and [`Eq`], if [`Self::equals`] returns true for two UDFs,
   941	    /// their `hash_value`s must be the same.
   942	    ///
   943	    /// By default, it only hashes the type. The other fields are not hashed, as usually the
   944	    /// name, signature, and aliases are implied by the UDF type. Recall that UDFs with state
   945	    /// (and thus possibly changing fields) must override [`Self::equals`] and [`Self::hash_value`].
   946	    fn hash_value(&self) -> u64 {
   947	        let hasher = &mut DefaultHasher::new();
   948	        self.as_any().type_id().hash(hasher);
   949	        hasher.finish()
   950	    }

    61	fn get_min_max_result_type(input_types: &[DataType]) -> Result<Vec<DataType>> {
    62	    // make sure that the input types only has one element.
    63	    if input_types.len() != 1 {
    64	        return exec_err!(
    65	            "min/max was called with {} arguments. It requires only 1.",
    66	            input_types.len()
    67	        );
    68	    }
    69	    // min and max support the dictionary data type
    70	    // unpack the dictionary to get the value
    71	    match &input_types[0] {
    72	        DataType::Dictionary(_, dict_value_type) => {
    73	            // TODO add checker, if the value type is complex data type
    74	            Ok(vec![dict_value_type.deref().clone()])
    75	        }
    76	        // TODO add checker for datatype which min and max supported
    77	        // For example, the `Struct` and `Map` type are not supported in the MIN and MAX function
    78	        _ => Ok(input_types.to_vec()),
    79	    }
    80	}

    82	#[user_doc(
    83	    doc_section(label = "General Functions"),
    84	    description = "Returns the maximum value in the specified column.",
    85	    syntax_example = "max(expression)",
    86	    sql_example = r#"```sql
    87	> SELECT max(column_name) FROM table_name;
    88	+----------------------+
    89	| max(column_name)      |
    90	+----------------------+
    91	| 150                  |
    92	+----------------------+
    93	```"#,
    94	    standard_argument(name = "expression",)
    95	)]
    96	// MAX aggregate UDF
    97	#[derive(Debug)]
    98	pub struct Max {
    99	    signature: Signature,
   100	}
   101	
   102	impl Max {
   103	    pub fn new() -> Self {
   104	        Self {
   105	            signature: Signature::user_defined(Volatility::Immutable),
   106	        }
   107	    }
   108	}
   109	
   110	impl Default for Max {
   111	    fn default() -> Self {
   112	        Self::new()
   113	    }
   114	}
   115	/// Creates a [`PrimitiveGroupsAccumulator`] for computing `MAX`
   116	/// the specified [`ArrowPrimitiveType`].
   117	///
   118	/// [`ArrowPrimitiveType`]: arrow::datatypes::ArrowPrimitiveType
   119	macro_rules! primitive_max_accumulator {
   120	    ($DATA_TYPE:ident, $NATIVE:ident, $PRIMTYPE:ident) => {{
   121	        Ok(Box::new(
   122	            PrimitiveGroupsAccumulator::<$PRIMTYPE, _>::new($DATA_TYPE, |cur, new| {
   123	                match (new).partial_cmp(cur) {
   124	                    Some(Ordering::Greater) | None => {
   125	                        // new is Greater or None
   126	                        *cur = new
   127	                    }
   128	                    _ => {}
   129	                }
   130	            })
   131	            // Initialize each accumulator to $NATIVE::MIN
   132	            .with_starting_value($NATIVE::MIN),
   133	        ))
   134	    }};
   135	}
   136	
   137	/// Creates a [`PrimitiveGroupsAccumulator`] for computing `MIN`
   138	/// the specified [`ArrowPrimitiveType`].
   139	///
   140	///
   141	/// [`ArrowPrimitiveType`]: arrow::datatypes::ArrowPrimitiveType
   142	macro_rules! primitive_min_accumulator {
   143	    ($DATA_TYPE:ident, $NATIVE:ident, $PRIMTYPE:ident) => {{
   144	        Ok(Box::new(
   145	            PrimitiveGroupsAccumulator::<$PRIMTYPE, _>::new(&$DATA_TYPE, |cur, new| {
   146	                match (new).partial_cmp(cur) {
   147	                    Some(Ordering::Less) | None => {
   148	                        // new is Less or NaN
   149	                        *cur = new
   150	                    }
   151	                    _ => {}
   152	                }
   153	            })
   154	            // Initialize each accumulator to $NATIVE::MAX
   155	            .with_starting_value($NATIVE::MAX),
   156	        ))
   157	    }};
   158	}
   159	
   160	trait FromColumnStatistics {
   161	    fn value_from_column_statistics(
   162	        &self,
   163	        stats: &ColumnStatistics,
   164	    ) -> Option<ScalarValue>;
   165	
   166	    fn value_from_statistics(
   167	        &self,
   168	        statistics_args: &StatisticsArgs,
   169	    ) -> Option<ScalarValue> {
   170	        if let Precision::Exact(num_rows) = &statistics_args.statistics.num_rows {
   171	            match *num_rows {
   172	                0 => return ScalarValue::try_from(statistics_args.return_type).ok(),
   173	                value if value > 0 => {
   174	                    let col_stats = &statistics_args.statistics.column_statistics;
   175	                    if statistics_args.exprs.len() == 1 {
   176	                        // TODO optimize with exprs other than Column
   177	                        if let Some(col_expr) = statistics_args.exprs[0]
   178	                            .as_any()
   179	                            .downcast_ref::<expressions::Column>()
   180	                        {
   181	                            return self.value_from_column_statistics(
   182	                                &col_stats[col_expr.index()],
   183	                            );
   184	                        }
   185	                    }
   186	                }
   187	                _ => {}
   188	            }
   189	        }
   190	        None
   191	    }
   192	}
   193	
   194	impl FromColumnStatistics for Max {
   195	    fn value_from_column_statistics(
   196	        &self,
   197	        col_stats: &ColumnStatistics,
   198	    ) -> Option<ScalarValue> {
   199	        if let Precision::Exact(ref val) = col_stats.max_value {
   200	            if !val.is_null() {
   201	                return Some(val.clone());
   202	            }
   203	        }
   204	        None
   205	    }
   206	}

   210	        self
   211	    }

   219	    }

   223	    }

   226	        Ok(Box::new(MaxAccumulator::try_new(
   227	            acc_args.return_field.data_type(),
   228	        )?))
   229	    }
   230	
   231	    fn groups_accumulator_supported(&self, args: AccumulatorArgs) -> bool {
   232	        use DataType::*;
   233	        matches!(
   234	            args.return_field.data_type(),
   235	            Int8 | Int16
   236	                | Int32
   237	                | Int64
   238	                | UInt8
   239	                | UInt16
   240	                | UInt32
   241	                | UInt64
   242	                | Float16
   243	                | Float32
   244	                | Float64
   245	                | Decimal128(_, _)
   246	                | Decimal256(_, _)
   247	                | Date32
   248	                | Date64
   249	                | Time32(_)
   250	                | Time64(_)
   251	                | Timestamp(_, _)
   252	                | Utf8
   253	                | LargeUtf8
   254	                | Utf8View
   255	                | Binary
   256	                | LargeBinary
   257	                | BinaryView
   258	                | Duration(_)
   259	                | Struct(_)
   260	        )
   261	    }
   262	
   263	    fn create_groups_accumulator(
   264	        &self,
   265	        args: AccumulatorArgs,
   266	    ) -> Result<Box<dyn GroupsAccumulator>> {
   267	        use DataType::*;
   268	        use TimeUnit::*;
   269	        let data_type = args.return_field.data_type();
   270	        match data_type {
   271	            Int8 => primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i8, Int8Type),
   272	            Int16 => primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i16, Int16Type),
   273	            Int32 => primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i32, Int32Type),
   274	            Int64 => primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i64, Int64Type),
   275	            UInt8 => primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, u8, UInt8Type),
   276	            UInt16 => primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, u16, UInt16Type),
   277	            UInt32 => primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, u32, UInt32Type),
   278	            UInt64 => primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, u64, UInt64Type),
   279	            Float16 => {
   280	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, f16, Float16Type)
   281	            }
   282	            Float32 => {
   283	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, f32, Float32Type)
   284	            }
   285	            Float64 => {
   286	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, f64, Float64Type)
   287	            }
   288	            Date32 => primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i32, Date32Type),
   289	            Date64 => primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i64, Date64Type),
   290	            Time32(Second) => {
   291	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i32, Time32SecondType)
   292	            }
   293	            Time32(Millisecond) => {
   294	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i32, Time32MillisecondType)
   295	            }
   296	            Time64(Microsecond) => {
   297	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i64, Time64MicrosecondType)
   298	            }
   299	            Time64(Nanosecond) => {
   300	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i64, Time64NanosecondType)
   301	            }
   302	            Timestamp(Second, _) => {
   303	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i64, TimestampSecondType)
   304	            }
   305	            Timestamp(Millisecond, _) => {
   306	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i64, TimestampMillisecondType)
   307	            }
   308	            Timestamp(Microsecond, _) => {
   309	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i64, TimestampMicrosecondType)
   310	            }
   311	            Timestamp(Nanosecond, _) => {
   312	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i64, TimestampNanosecondType)
   313	            }
   314	            Duration(Second) => {
   315	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i64, DurationSecondType)
   316	            }
   317	            Duration(Millisecond) => {
   318	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i64, DurationMillisecondType)
   319	            }
   320	            Duration(Microsecond) => {
   321	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i64, DurationMicrosecondType)
   322	            }
   323	            Duration(Nanosecond) => {
   324	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i64, DurationNanosecondType)
   325	            }
   326	            Decimal128(_, _) => {
   327	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i128, Decimal128Type)
   328	            }
   329	            Decimal256(_, _) => {
   330	                primitive_max_accumulator!(data_type, i256, Decimal256Type)
   331	            }
   332	            Utf8 | LargeUtf8 | Utf8View | Binary | LargeBinary | BinaryView => {
   333	                Ok(Box::new(MinMaxBytesAccumulator::new_max(data_type.clone())))
   334	            }
   335	            Struct(_) => Ok(Box::new(MinMaxStructAccumulator::new_max(
   336	                data_type.clone(),
   337	            ))),
   338	            // This is only reached if groups_accumulator_supported is out of sync
   339	            _ => internal_err!("GroupsAccumulator not supported for max({})", data_type),
   340	        }
   341	    }

   381	macro_rules! min_max_generic {
   382	    ($VALUE:expr, $DELTA:expr, $OP:ident) => {{
   383	        if $VALUE.is_null() {
   384	            let mut delta_copy = $DELTA.clone();
   385	            // When the new value won we want to compact it to
   386	            // avoid storing the entire input
   387	            delta_copy.compact();
   388	            delta_copy
   389	        } else if $DELTA.is_null() {
   390	            $VALUE.clone()
   391	        } else {
   392	            match $VALUE.partial_cmp(&$DELTA) {
   393	                Some(choose_min_max!($OP)) => {
   394	                    // When the new value won we want to compact it to
   395	                    // avoid storing the entire input
   396	                    let mut delta_copy = $DELTA.clone();
   397	                    delta_copy.compact();
   398	                    delta_copy
   399	                }
   400	                _ => $VALUE.clone(),
   401	            }
   402	        }
   403	    }};
   404	}
   405	
   406	// min/max of two non-string scalar values.
   407	macro_rules! typed_min_max {
   408	    ($VALUE:expr, $DELTA:expr, $SCALAR:ident, $OP:ident $(, $EXTRA_ARGS:ident)*) => {{
   409	        ScalarValue::$SCALAR(
   410	            match ($VALUE, $DELTA) {
   411	                (None, None) => None,
   412	                (Some(a), None) => Some(*a),
   413	                (None, Some(b)) => Some(*b),
   414	                (Some(a), Some(b)) => Some((*a).$OP(*b)),
   415	            },
   416	            $($EXTRA_ARGS.clone()),*
   417	        )
   418	    }};
   419	}
   420	macro_rules! typed_min_max_float {
   421	    ($VALUE:expr, $DELTA:expr, $SCALAR:ident, $OP:ident) => {{
   422	        ScalarValue::$SCALAR(match ($VALUE, $DELTA) {
   423	            (None, None) => None,
   424	            (Some(a), None) => Some(*a),
   425	            (None, Some(b)) => Some(*b),
   426	            (Some(a), Some(b)) => match a.total_cmp(b) {
   427	                choose_min_max!($OP) => Some(*b),
   428	                _ => Some(*a),
   429	            },
   430	        })
   431	    }};
   432	}
   433	
   434	// min/max of two scalar string values.
   435	macro_rules! typed_min_max_string {
   436	    ($VALUE:expr, $DELTA:expr, $SCALAR:ident, $OP:ident) => {{
   437	        ScalarValue::$SCALAR(match ($VALUE, $DELTA) {
   438	            (None, None) => None,
   439	            (Some(a), None) => Some(a.clone()),
   440	            (None, Some(b)) => Some(b.clone()),
   441	            (Some(a), Some(b)) => Some((a).$OP(b).clone()),
   442	        })
   443	    }};
   444	}

   449	        ScalarValue::$SCALAR(
   450	            $ARG,
   451	            match ($VALUE, $DELTA) {
   452	                (None, None) => None,
   453	                (Some(a), None) => Some(a.clone()),

import os
import re

# Directory containing the UDAF implementations
udaf_dir = "/testbed/repo/datafusion/functions-aggregate/src"

# Pattern to find struct definitions that implement AggregateUDFImpl
struct_pattern = re.compile(r'"'"'^pub struct (\w+)\s*{'"'"', re.MULTILINE)
implement_pattern = re.compile(r'"'"'^impl AggregateUDFImpl for (\w+)'"'"', re.MULTILINE)

derive_pattern = re.compile(r'"'"'^#\[derive\([^)]*PartialEq[^)]*\)\]'"'"', re.MULTILINE)
derive_hash_pattern = re.compile(r'"'"'^#\[derive\([^)]*Hash[^)]*\)\]'"'"', re.MULTILINE)

udaf_structs = []
missing_partial_eq = []
missing_hash = []

# Iterate through all Rust files in the directory
for filename in os.listdir(udaf_dir):
    if filename.endswith('"'"'.rs'"'"'):
        filepath = os.path.join(udaf_dir, filename)
        with open(filepath, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
            content = f.read()
            
        # Find all struct definitions
        struct_matches = struct_pattern.findall(content)
        
        # Find which structs implement AggregateUDFImpl
        for struct_name in struct_matches:
            if f"impl AggregateUDFImpl for {struct_name}" in content:
                udaf_structs.append((filename, struct_name))
                
                # Check if PartialEq is derived
                start_pos = content.find(f"pub struct {struct_name}")
                if start_pos != -1:
                    # Look backwards for derive attributes
                    line_start = content.rfind('"'"'\n'"'"', 0, start_pos) + 1
                    prev_lines = content[line_start:start_pos]
                    
                    if not derive_pattern.search(prev_lines):
                        missing_partial_eq.append((filename, struct_name))
                    
                    if not derive_hash_pattern.search(prev_lines):
                        missing_hash.append((filename, struct_name))

print("UDAF structs that implement AggregateUDFImpl:")
for filename, struct_name in udaf_structs:
    print(f"  {filename}: {struct_name}")

print("\nUDAF structs missing PartialEq derive:")
for filename, struct_name in missing_partial_eq:
    print(f"  {filename}: {struct_name}")

print("\nUDAF structs missing Hash derive:")
for filename, struct_name in missing_hash:
    print(f"  {filename}: {struct_name}")

print(f"\nTotal UDAF structs: {len(udaf_structs)}")
print(f"Missing PartialEq: {len(missing_partial_eq)}")
print(f"Missing Hash: {len(missing_hash)}")'

Based on my analysis, I understand the requirements:

1. **All UDAF structs** that implement `AggregateUDFImpl` need to have `PartialEq` and `Hash` traits implemented.
2. The PR description states this should be done by adding `#[derive(PartialEq, Hash)]` to all of them.
3. Some files already use `udf_equals_hash!(AggregateUDFImpl);` macro, which provides default implementations for `equals` and `hash_value` methods.

import os
import re

# Directory containing the UDAF implementations
udaf_dir = "/testbed/repo/datafusion/functions-aggregate/src"

# Pattern to find struct definitions that implement AggregateUDFImpl
struct_pattern = re.compile(r'"'"'^(#[^\n]*\n)*pub struct (\w+)\s*{'"'"', re.MULTILINE)
implement_pattern = re.compile(r'"'"'^impl AggregateUDFImpl for (\w+)'"'"', re.MULTILINE)

derive_pattern = re.compile(r'"'"'^#\[derive\([^)]*\]\s*\n)'"'"', re.MULTILINE)

# List of files that need modification
files_to_modify = []

# Iterate through all Rust files in the directory
for filename in os.listdir(udaf_dir):
    if filename.endswith('"'"'.rs'"'"'):
        filepath = os.path.join(udaf_dir, filename)
        with open(filepath, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
            content = f.read()
            
        # Find all struct definitions
        struct_matches = list(struct_pattern.finditer(content))
        
        # Get all structs that implement AggregateUDFImpl
        udaf_structs = []
        for match in struct_matches:
            struct_name = match.group(2)
            if f"impl AggregateUDFImpl for {struct_name}" in content:
                udaf_structs.append((match.start(), match.group(0), struct_name))
        
        # Check if PartialEq and Hash are already in the derive list
        for start_pos, struct_def, struct_name in udaf_structs:
            # Look at the lines immediately before the struct definition
            line_start = content.rfind('"'"'\n'"'"', 0, start_pos) + 1
            prev_lines = content[line_start:start_pos]
            
            # Check if PartialEq and Hash are already derived
            has_partial_eq = "PartialEq" in prev_lines
            has_hash = "Hash" in prev_lines
            
            if not has_partial_eq or not has_hash:
                files_to_modify.append((filename, struct_name, struct_def, start_pos, has_partial_eq, has_hash))

# Now modify the files
for filename, struct_name, struct_def, start_pos, has_partial_eq, has_hash in files_to_modify:
    filepath = os.path.join(udaf_dir, filename)
    
    with open(filepath, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # Find the struct definition and its derive attributes
    line_start = content.rfind('"'"'\n'"'"', 0, start_pos) + 1
    struct_full_def = content[line_start:start_pos + len(struct_def)]
    
    print(f"\n=== {filename}: {struct_name} ===")
    print(f"Current struct definition:")
    print(struct_full_def)
    
    # Check if there'"'"'s already a derive attribute
    if "#[derive(" in struct_full_def:
        # Modify existing derive attribute
        derive_match = re.search(r'"'"'(#\[derive\()([^)]*)(\)\])'"'"', struct_full_def)
        if derive_match:
            current_derives = derive_match.group(2)
            new_derives = current_derives
            
            if not has_partial_eq:
                new_derives += ", PartialEq"
            if not has_hash:
                new_derives += ", Hash"
            
            new_struct_def = struct_full_def.replace(
                f"#[derive({current_derives})]",
                f"#[derive({new_derives})]"
            )
    else:
        # Add new derive attribute
        new_derives = "Debug"
        if not has_partial_eq:
            new_derives += ", PartialEq"
        if not has_hash:
            new_derives += ", Hash"
        
        new_struct_def = f"#[derive({new_derives})]\n{struct_def}"
    
    # Replace the content
    new_content = content[:line_start] + new_struct_def + content[start_pos + len(struct_def):]
    
    # Write back to file
    with open(filepath, '"'"'w'"'"') as f:
        f.write(new_content)
    
    print(f"Modified struct definition:")
    print(new_struct_def)

print(f"\nModified {len(files_to_modify)} structs across {len(set(f[0] for f in files_to_modify))} files")'

import os
import re

# Directory containing the UDAF implementations
udaf_dir = "/testbed/repo/datafusion/functions-aggregate/src"

# Iterate through all Rust files in the directory
for filename in os.listdir(udaf_dir):
    if filename.endswith('"'"'.rs'"'"'):
        filepath = os.path.join(udaf_dir, filename)
        with open(filepath, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
            content = f.read()
        
        # Find all struct definitions that have AggregateUDFImpl implementations
        # Look for patterns like "pub struct Name { ... }" followed by "impl AggregateUDFImpl for Name"
        
        # Simple approach: find all structs and check if they have AggregateUDFImpl implementations
        lines = content.split('"'"'\n'"'"')
        modified = False
        
        for i, line in enumerate(lines):
            if line.strip().startswith('"'"'pub struct '"'"') and '"'"'{'"'"' in line:
                # Extract struct name
                struct_name = line.split('"'"'struct '"'"')[1].split('"'"' {'"'"')[0].strip()
                
                # Check if this struct has an AggregateUDFImpl implementation
                if f"impl AggregateUDFImpl for {struct_name}" in content:
                    # Look backwards for derive attributes
                    j = i - 1
                    found_derive = False
                    while j >= 0:
                        if lines[j].strip().startswith('"'"'#[derive('"'"'):
                            # Check if PartialEq and Hash are already there
                            if '"'"'PartialEq'"'"' not in lines[j] or '"'"'Hash'"'"' not in lines[j]:
                                # Add missing traits
                                new_derive = lines[j].replace('"'"']'"'"', '"'"', PartialEq, Hash]'"'"')
                                lines[j] = new_derive
                                print(f"Modified {filename}: {struct_name}")
                                modified = True
                            found_derive = True
                            break
                        elif lines[j].strip() == '"'"''"'"':
                            j -= 1
                        else:
                            # No derive attribute found, add one
                            lines.insert(i, '"'"'#[derive(Debug, PartialEq, Hash)]'"'"')
                            print(f"Added derive to {filename}: {struct_name}")
                            modified = True
                            break
                    
                    if not found_derive and j < 0:
                        # No derive attribute found at all
                        lines.insert(i, '"'"'#[derive(Debug, PartialEq, Hash)]'"'"')
                        print(f"Added derive to {filename}: {struct_name}")
                        modified = True
        
        if modified:
            # Write back to file
            with open(filepath, '"'"'w'"'"') as f:
                f.write('"'"'\n'"'"'.join(lines))

import os
import re

# Directory containing the UDAF implementations
udaf_dir = "/testbed/repo/datafusion/functions-aggregate/src"

# Pattern to fix incorrect derive syntax

incorrect_derive_pattern = re.compile(r'"'"'#\[derive\((.*?)\),\s*(PartialEq|Hash)\s*,\s*(PartialEq|Hash)\]'"'"')

# Fix files

    if filename.endswith('"'"'.rs'"'"'):
        filepath = os.path.join(udaf_dir, filename)
        
        with open(filepath, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
            content = f.read()
        
        # Search for incorrect patterns
        matches = list(incorrect_derive_pattern.finditer(content))
        
        if matches:
            print(f"Fixing {filename}")

                entire_match = match.group(0)
                inner_content = match.group(1)

                    fixed_derive = f"#[derive({fixed_traits})]"

str_replace_editor create /testbed/repo/verify_udaf_derives.py --file_text '#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os
import re

# Directory containing the UDAF implementations
udaf_dir = "/testbed/repo/datafusion/functions-aggregate/src"

# Pattern to find struct definitions that implement AggregateUDFImpl
struct_pattern = re.compile(r'"'"'^#[^\n]*derive[^\n]*\npub struct (\w+)\s*{'"'"', re.MULTILINE)

results = {}

# Iterate through all Rust files in the directory
for filename in os.listdir(udaf_dir):
    if filename.endswith('"'"'.rs'"'"'):
        filepath = os.path.join(udaf_dir, filename)
        with open(filepath, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
            content = f.read()
        
        # Find all struct definitions with derives
        struct_matches = list(struct_pattern.finditer(content))
        
        for match in struct_matches:
            struct_full_line = match.group(0)
            struct_name = match.group(1)
            
            # Check if this struct implements AggregateUDFImpl
            if f"impl AggregateUDFImpl for {struct_name}" in content:
                has_partial_eq = "PartialEq" in struct_full_line
                has_hash = "Hash" in struct_full_line
                
                results[f"{filename}:{struct_name}"] = {
                    '"'"'full_line'"'"': struct_full_line.strip(),
                    '"'"'has_partial_eq'"'"': has_partial_eq,
                    '"'"'has_hash'"'"': has_hash
                }

print("UDAF structs with derives:")
for key, info in results.items():
    print(f"\n{key}:")
    print(f"  Derive line: {info['"'"'full_line'"'"']}")
    print(f"  Has PartialEq: {info['"'"'has_partial_eq'"'"']}")
    print(f"  Has Hash: {info['"'"'has_hash'"'"']}")

print(f"\nTotal checked: {len(results)}")'

use std::collections::HashSet;
use std::hash::{Hash, Hasher};

fn main() {
    let functions = all_default_aggregate_functions();
    
    println!("Testing {} UDAF functions:", functions.len());
    
    // Test that we can hash the functions
    let mut hashes = HashSet::new();
    
    for func in &functions {
        let mut hasher = std::collections::hash_map::DefaultHasher::new();
        func.hash(&mut hasher);
        let hash = hasher.finish();
        
        println!("  {}: hash = {}", func.name(), hash);
        
        // Check that we can insert into a HashSet
        hashes.insert(func.name().to_string());
    }
    
    // Test equality between functions
    println!("\nTesting equality:");
    for (i, func1) in functions.iter().enumerate() {
        for (j, func2) in functions.iter().enumerate() {
            if i == j {
                // Should be equal to itself
                assert!(func1 == func2, "Function should be equal to itself");
            } else if func1.name() == func2.name() {
                // Functions with same name should be equal
                assert!(func1 == func2, "Functions with same name should be equal");
            }
        }
    }
    
    println!("\nAll tests passed! UDAF functions now implement PartialEq and Hash correctly.");
}'

diff --git a/add_udaf_derives.py b/add_udaf_derives.py
new file mode 100644
index 000000000..e863e9e7f
--- /dev/null
+++ b/add_udaf_derives.py
@@ -0,0 +1,63 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+import os
+import re
+
+# Directory containing the UDAF implementations
+udaf_dir = "/testbed/repo/datafusion/functions-aggregate/src"
+
+# Iterate through all Rust files in the directory
+for filename in os.listdir(udaf_dir):
+    if filename.endswith('.rs'):
+        filepath = os.path.join(udaf_dir, filename)
+        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
+            content = f.read()
+        
+        # Find all struct definitions that have AggregateUDFImpl implementations
+        # Look for patterns like "pub struct Name { ... }" followed by "impl AggregateUDFImpl for Name"
+        
+        # Simple approach: find all structs and check if they have AggregateUDFImpl implementations
+        lines = content.split('\n')
+        modified = False
+        
+        for i, line in enumerate(lines):
+            if line.strip().startswith('pub struct ') and '{' in line:
+                # Extract struct name
+                struct_name = line.split('struct ')[1].split(' {')[0].strip()
+                
+                # Check if this struct has an AggregateUDFImpl implementation
+                if f"impl AggregateUDFImpl for {struct_name}" in content:
+                    # Look backwards for derive attributes
+                    j = i - 1
+                    found_derive = False
+                    while j >= 0:
+                        if lines[j].strip().startswith('#[derive('):
+                            # Check if PartialEq and Hash are already there
+                            if 'PartialEq' not in lines[j] or 'Hash' not in lines[j]:
+                                # Add missing traits
+                                new_derive = lines[j].replace(']', ', PartialEq, Hash]')
+                                lines[j] = new_derive
+                                print(f"Modified {filename}: {struct_name}")
+                                modified = True
+                            found_derive = True
+                            break
+                        elif lines[j].strip() == '':
+                            j -= 1
+                        else:
+                            # No derive attribute found, add one
+                            lines.insert(i, '#[derive(Debug, PartialEq, Hash)]')
+                            print(f"Added derive to {filename}: {struct_name}")
+                            modified = True
+                            break
+                    
+                    if not found_derive and j < 0:
+                        # No derive attribute found at all
+                        lines.insert(i, '#[derive(Debug, PartialEq, Hash)]')
+                        print(f"Added derive to {filename}: {struct_name}")
+                        modified = True
+        
+        if modified:
+            # Write back to file
+            with open(filepath, 'w') as f:
+                f.write('\n'.join(lines))
+
+print("\nCompleted adding PartialEq and Hash derives to UDAF structs.")
\ No newline at end of file
diff --git a/check_udaf_derives.py b/check_udaf_derives.py
new file mode 100644
index 000000000..cdc79de58
--- /dev/null
+++ b/check_udaf_derives.py
@@ -0,0 +1,61 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+import os
+import re
+
+# Directory containing the UDAF implementations
+udaf_dir = "/testbed/repo/datafusion/functions-aggregate/src"
+
+# Pattern to find struct definitions that implement AggregateUDFImpl
+struct_pattern = re.compile(r'^pub struct (\w+)\s*{', re.MULTILINE)
+implement_pattern = re.compile(r'^impl AggregateUDFImpl for (\w+)', re.MULTILINE)
+
+derive_pattern = re.compile(r'^#\[derive\([^)]*PartialEq[^)]*\)\]', re.MULTILINE)
+derive_hash_pattern = re.compile(r'^#\[derive\([^)]*Hash[^)]*\)\]', re.MULTILINE)
+
+udaf_structs = []
+missing_partial_eq = []
+missing_hash = []
+
+# Iterate through all Rust files in the directory
+for filename in os.listdir(udaf_dir):
+    if filename.endswith('.rs'):
+        filepath = os.path.join(udaf_dir, filename)
+        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
+            content = f.read()
+            
+        # Find all struct definitions
+        struct_matches = struct_pattern.findall(content)
+        
+        # Find which structs implement AggregateUDFImpl
+        for struct_name in struct_matches:
+            if f"impl AggregateUDFImpl for {struct_name}" in content:
+                udaf_structs.append((filename, struct_name))
+                
+                # Check if PartialEq is derived
+                start_pos = content.find(f"pub struct {struct_name}")
+                if start_pos != -1:
+                    # Look backwards for derive attributes
+                    line_start = content.rfind('\n', 0, start_pos) + 1
+                    prev_lines = content[line_start:start_pos]
+                    
+                    if not derive_pattern.search(prev_lines):
+                        missing_partial_eq.append((filename, struct_name))
+                    
+                    if not derive_hash_pattern.search(prev_lines):
+                        missing_hash.append((filename, struct_name))
+
+print("UDAF structs that implement AggregateUDFImpl:")
+for filename, struct_name in udaf_structs:
+    print(f"  {filename}: {struct_name}")
+
+print("\nUDAF structs missing PartialEq derive:")
+for filename, struct_name in missing_partial_eq:
+    print(f"  {filename}: {struct_name}")
+
+print("\nUDAF structs missing Hash derive:")
+for filename, struct_name in missing_hash:
+    print(f"  {filename}: {struct_name}")
+
+print(f"\nTotal UDAF structs: {len(udaf_structs)}")
+print(f"Missing PartialEq: {len(missing_partial_eq)}")
+print(f"Missing Hash: {len(missing_hash)}")
\ No newline at end of file

diff --git a/fix_udaf_derives.py b/fix_udaf_derives.py
new file mode 100644
index 000000000..94a838410
--- /dev/null
+++ b/fix_udaf_derives.py
@@ -0,0 +1,56 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+import os
+import re
+
+# Directory containing the UDAF implementations
+udaf_dir = "/testbed/repo/datafusion/functions-aggregate/src"
+
+# Pattern to fix incorrect derive syntax
+derive_fix_pattern = re.compile(r'#\[derive\((.*?)\)\s*,\s*(PartialEq|Hash)\s*,\s*(PartialEq|Hash)\]')
+incorrect_derive_pattern = re.compile(r'#\[derive\((.*?)\),\s*(PartialEq|Hash)\s*,\s*(PartialEq|Hash)\]')
+
+# Fix files
+for filename in os.listdir(udaf_dir):
+    if filename.endswith('.rs'):
+        filepath = os.path.join(udaf_dir, filename)
+        
+        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
+            content = f.read()
+        
+        # Search for incorrect patterns
+        matches = list(incorrect_derive_pattern.finditer(content))
+        
+        if matches:
+            print(f"Fixing {filename}")
+            
+            for match in reversed(matches):  # Reverse to avoid index shifting issues
+                entire_match = match.group(0)
+                inner_content = match.group(1)
+                traits = match.captures.tuple() if hasattr(match, 'captures') else match.groups()
+                
+                # Fix the syntax
+                if len(traits) >= 3:
+                    fixed_traits = f"{inner_content}, {traits[1]}, {traits[2]}"
+                    fixed_derive = f"#[derive({fixed_traits})]"
+                    
+                    content = content[:match.start()] + fixed_derive + content[match.end():]
+            
+            # Write back to file
+            with open(filepath, 'w') as f:
+                f.write(content)
+
+# Also fix the specific case we saw
+filepath = "/testbed/repo/datafusion/functions-aggregate/src/average.rs"
+with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
+    content = f.read()
+
+# Fix the specific pattern we saw
+content = content.replace(
+    "#[derive(Debug), PartialEq, Hash]",
+    "#[derive(Debug, PartialEq, Hash)]"
+)
+
+with open(filepath, 'w') as f:
+    f.write(content)
+
+print("Fixed derive syntax")
\ No newline at end of file

+use datafusion_functions_aggregate::all_default_aggregate_functions;
+use std::collections::HashSet;
+use std::hash::{Hash, Hasher};
+
+fn main() {
+    let functions = all_default_aggregate_functions();
+    
+    println!("Testing {} UDAF functions:", functions.len());
+    
+    // Test that we can hash the functions
+    let mut hashes = HashSet::new();
+    
+    for func in &functions {
+        let mut hasher = std::collections::hash_map::DefaultHasher::new();
+        func.hash(&mut hasher);
+        let hash = hasher.finish();
+        
+        println!("  {}: hash = {}", func.name(), hash);
+        
+        // Check that we can insert into a HashSet
+        hashes.insert(func.name().to_string());
+    }
+    
+    // Test equality between functions
+    println!("\nTesting equality:");
+    for (i, func1) in functions.iter().enumerate() {
+        for (j, func2) in functions.iter().enumerate() {
+            if i == j {
+                // Should be equal to itself
+                assert!(func1 == func2, "Function should be equal to itself");
+            } else if func1.name() == func2.name() {
+                // Functions with same name should be equal
+                assert!(func1 == func2, "Functions with same name should be equal");
+            }
+        }
+    }
+    
+    println!("\nAll tests passed! UDAF functions now implement PartialEq and Hash correctly.");
+}

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+import os
+import re
+
+# Directory containing the UDAF implementations
+udaf_dir = "/testbed/repo/datafusion/functions-aggregate/src"
+
+# Pattern to find struct definitions that implement AggregateUDFImpl
+struct_pattern = re.compile(r'^#[^\n]*derive[^\n]*\npub struct (\w+)\s*{', re.MULTILINE)
+
+results = {}
+
+# Iterate through all Rust files in the directory
+for filename in os.listdir(udaf_dir):
+    if filename.endswith('.rs'):
+        filepath = os.path.join(udaf_dir, filename)
+        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
+            content = f.read()
+        
+        # Find all struct definitions with derives
+        struct_matches = list(struct_pattern.finditer(content))
+        
+        for match in struct_matches:
+            struct_full_line = match.group(0)
+            struct_name = match.group(1)
+            
+            # Check if this struct implements AggregateUDFImpl
+            if f"impl AggregateUDFImpl for {struct_name}" in content:
+                has_partial_eq = "PartialEq" in struct_full_line
+                has_hash = "Hash" in struct_full_line
+                
+                results[f"{filename}:{struct_name}"] = {
+                    'full_line': struct_full_line.strip(),
+                    'has_partial_eq': has_partial_eq,
+                    'has_hash': has_hash
+                }
+
+print("UDAF structs with derives:")
+for key, info in results.items():
+    print(f"\n{key}:")
+    print(f"  Derive line: {info['full_line']}")
+    print(f"  Has PartialEq: {info['has_partial_eq']}")
+    print(f"  Has Hash: {info['has_hash']}")
+
+print(f"\nTotal checked: {len(results)}")
\ No newline at end of file

</diff>
